<div class="tit"><h2> </h2>
<h1> 中华人民共和国网络安全法</h1>
<h3> （2016年11月7日第十二届全国人民代表大会常务委员会第二十四次会议通过）</h3>
<p></p>
</div>

<div class="fontsize"><span class="fr">浏览字号： <a href="#" onclick="Zoom.style.fontSize='24px';">大</a> <a href="#" onclick="Zoom.style.fontSize='16px';">中</a> <a href="#" onclick="Zoom.style.fontSize='12px';">小</a></span> 来源： 中国人大网 2016年11月7日 17:31:34</div>

<div id="Zoom"><!--enpproperty <date>2016-11-07 17:31:34.0</date><author></author><title>中华人民共和国网络安全法</title><keyword></keyword><subtitle>（2016年11月7日第十二届全国人民代表大会常务委员会第二十四次会议通过）</subtitle><introtitle></introtitle><siteid>1</siteid><nodeid>33635</nodeid><nodename>相关资料</nodename><nodesearchname></nodesearchname>/enpproperty--><!--enpcontent--> <p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: center; mso-layout-grid-align: none" class="MsoNormal" align="center"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZHTK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体">目    录<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-layout-grid-align: none" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZKTK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">    第一章  总    则<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-layout-grid-align: none" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZKTK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">    第二章  网络安全支持与促进<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-layout-grid-align: none" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZKTK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">    第三章  网络运行安全<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZKTK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">    第一节  一般规定<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZKTK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">    第二节  关键信息基础设施的运行安全<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-layout-grid-align: none" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZKTK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">    第四章  网络信息安全<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-layout-grid-align: none" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZKTK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">    第五章  监测预警与应急处置<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-layout-grid-align: none" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZKTK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">    第六章  法律责任<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZKTK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">    第七章  附    则<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: center" class="MsoNormal" align="center"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZHTK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体">第一章  总    则</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZKTK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体" lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZHTK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第一条</span></b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZHTK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">  </span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">为了保障网络安全</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">维护网络空间主权和国家安全</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">社会公共利益</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">保护公民</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">法人和其他组织的合法权益</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">促进经济社会信息化健康发展</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">制定本法</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.5pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.95" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZHTK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第二条</span></b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZHTK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">  </span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">在中华人民共和国境内建设</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">运营</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">维护和使用网络</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">以及网络安全的监督管理</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">适用本法</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZHTK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第三条</span></b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZHTK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">  </span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">国家坚持网络安全与信息化发展并重</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">遵循积极利用</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">科学发展</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">依法管理</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">确保安全的方针</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">推进网络基础设施</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">建设和互联互通</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">鼓励网络技术创新和应用</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">支持培养网络安全人才</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">建立健全网络安全保障体系</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">提高网络安全保护能力</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZHTK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第四条</span></b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZHTK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">  </span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">国家制定并不断完善网络安全战略</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">明确保障网络安全的基本要求和主要目标</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">提出重点领域的网络安全政策</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">工作任务和措施</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZHTK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第五条</span></b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZHTK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">  </span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">国家采取措施</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">监测</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">防御</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">处置来源于中华人民共和国境内外的网络安全风险和威胁</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">保护关键信息基础设施免受攻击</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">侵入</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">干扰和破坏</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">依法惩治网络违法犯罪活动</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">维护网络空间安全和秩序</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZHTK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第六条</span></b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZHTK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">  </span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">国家倡导诚实守信</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">健康文明的网络行为</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">推动传播社会主义核心价值观</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">采取措施提高全社会的网络安全意识和水平</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">形成全社会共同参与促进网络安全的良好环境</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZHTK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第七条</span></b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZHTK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">  </span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">国家积极开展网络空间治理</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">网络技术研发和标准制定</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">打击网络违法犯罪等方面的国际交流与合作</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">推动构建和平</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">安全</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">开放</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">合作的网络空间</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">建立多边</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">民主</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">透明的网络治理体系</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZHTK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第八条 </span></b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZHTK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">&#160;</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">国家网信部门负责统筹协调网络安全工作和相关监督管理工作</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">国务院电信主管部门</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">公安部门和其他有关机关依照本法和有关法律</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">行政法规的规定</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">在各自职责范围内负责网络安全保护和监督管理工作</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.5pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">县级以上地方人民政府有关部门的网络安全保护和监督管理职责</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">按照国家有关规定确定</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZHTK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第九条 </span></b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZHTK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">&#160;</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">网络运营者开展经营和服务活动</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">必须遵守法律</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">行政法规</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">尊重社会公德</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">遵守商业道德</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">诚实信用</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">履行网络安全保护义务</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">接受政府和社会的监督</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">承担社会责任</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZHTK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第十条</span></b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZHTK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">  </span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">建设</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">运营网络或者通过网络提供服务</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">应当依照法律</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">行政法规的规定和国家标准的强制性要求</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">采取技术措施和其他必要措施</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">保障网络安全</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">稳定运行</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">有效应对网络安全事件</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">防范网络违法犯罪活动</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">维护网络数据的完整性</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">保密性和可用性</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第十一条 </span></b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"> 网络相关行业组织按照章程</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">加强行业自律</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">制定网络安全行为规范</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">指导会员加强网络安全保护</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">提高网络安全保护水平</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">促进行业健康发展</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第十二条 </span></b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"> 国家保护公民</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">法人和其他组织依法使用网络的权利</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">促进网络接入普及</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">提升网络服务水平</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">为社会提供安全</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">便利的网络服务</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">保障网络信息依法有序自由流动</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.5pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">任何个人和组织使用网络应当遵守宪法法律</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">遵守公共秩序</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">尊重社会公德</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">不得危害网络安全</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">不得利用网络从事危害国家安全</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">荣誉和利益</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">煽动颠覆国家政权</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">推翻社会主义制度</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">煽动分裂国家</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">破坏国家统一</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">宣扬恐怖主义</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">极端主义</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">宣扬民族仇恨</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">民族歧视</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">传播暴力</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">淫秽色情信息</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">编造</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">传播虚假信息扰乱经济秩序和社会秩序</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">以及侵害他人名誉</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">隐私</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">知识产权和其他合法权益等活动</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第十三条 </span></b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"> 国家支持研究开发有利于未成年人健康成长的网络产品和服务</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">依法惩治利用网络从事危害未成年人身心健康的活动</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">为未成年人提供安全</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">健康的网络环境</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第十四条 </span></b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"> 任何个人和组织有权对危害网络安全的行为向网信</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">电信</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">公安等部门举报</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">收到举报的部门应当及时依法作出处理</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">；</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">不属于本部门职责的</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">应当及时移送有权处理的部门</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.5pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">有关部门应当对举报人的相关信息予以保密</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">保护举报人的合法权益</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: center; mso-layout-grid-align: none" class="MsoNormal" align="center"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体">第二章  网络安全支持与促进<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第十五条 </span></b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"> 国家建立和完善网络安全标准体系</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">国务院标准化行政主管部门和国务院其他有关部门根据各自的职责</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">组织制定并适时修订有关网络安全管理以及网络产品</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">服务和运行安全的国家标准</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">行业标准</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.5pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">国家支持企业</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">研究机构</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">高等学校</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">网络相关行业组织参与网络安全国家标准</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">行业标准的制定</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第十六条</span></b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">  国务院和省</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">自治区</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">直辖市人民政府应当统筹规划</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">加大投入</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">扶持重点网络安全技术产业和项目</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">支持网络安全技术的研究开发和应用</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">推广安全可信的网络产品和服务</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">保护网络技术知识产权</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">支持企业</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">研究机构和高等学校等参与国家网络安全技术创新项目</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第十七条</span></b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">  国家推进网络安全社会化服务体系建设</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">鼓励有关企业</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">机构开展网络安全认证</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">检测和风险评估等安全服务</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第十八条</span></b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">  国家鼓励开发网络数据安全保护和利用技术</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">促进公共数据资源开放</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">推动技术创新和经济社会发展</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.5pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">国家支持创新网络安全管理方式</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">运用网络新技术</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">提升网络安全保护水平</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第十九条</span></b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">  各级人民政府及其有关部门应当组织开展经常性的网络安全宣传教育</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">并指导</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">督促有关单位做好网络安全宣传教育工作</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.5pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">大众传播媒介应当有针对性地面向社会进行网络安全宣传教育</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第二十条 </span></b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"> 国家支持企业和高等学校</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">职业学校等教育培训机构开展网络安全相关教育与培训</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">采取多种方式培养网络安全人才</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">促进网络安全人才交流</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: center; mso-layout-grid-align: none" class="MsoNormal" align="center"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体">第三章  网络运行安全<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: center; mso-layout-grid-align: none" class="MsoNormal" align="center"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 华文楷体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZKTK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"><font face="楷体_GB2312">第一节 一般规定<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></font></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第二十一条 </span></b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"> 国家实行网络安全等级保护制度</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">网络运营者应当按照网络安全等级保护制度的要求</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">履行下列安全保护义务</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">保障网络免受干扰</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">破坏或者未经授权的访问</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">防止网络数据泄露或者被窃取</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">篡改</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">：<span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.5pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">（</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">一</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">）</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">制定内部安全管理制度和操作规程</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">确定网络安全负责人</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">落实网络安全保护责任</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">；<span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">（</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">二</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">）</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">采取防范计算机病毒和网络攻击</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">网络侵入等危害网络安全行为的技术措施</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">；<span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">（</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">三</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">）</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">采取监测</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">记录网络运行状态</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">网络安全事件的技术措施</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">并按照规定留存相关的网络日志不少于六个月</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">；<span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">（</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">四</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">）</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">采取数据分类</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">重要数据备份和加密等措施</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">；<span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">（</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">五</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">）</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">法律</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">行政法规规定的其他义务</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第二十二条 </span></b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"> 网络产品</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">服务应当符合相关国家标准的强制性要求</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">网络产品</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">服务的提供者不得设置恶意程序</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">；</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">发现其网络产品</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">服务存在安全缺陷</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">漏洞等风险时</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">应当立即采取补救措施</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">按照规定及时告知用户并向有关主管部门报告</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.5pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">网络产品</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">服务的提供者应当为其产品</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">服务持续提供安全维护</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">；</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">在规定或者当事人约定的期限内</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">不得终止提供安全维护</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.5pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">网络产品</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">服务具有收集用户信息功能的</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">其提供者应当向用户明示并取得同意</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">；</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">涉及用户个人信息的</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">还应当遵守本法和有关法律</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">行政法规关于个人信息保护的规定</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第二十三条 </span></b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"> 网络关键设备和网络安全专用产品应当按照相关国家标准的强制性要求</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">由具备资格的机构安全认证合格或者安全检测符合要求后</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">方可销售或者提供</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">国家网信部门会同国务院有关部门制定</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">公布网络关键设备和网络安全专用产品目录</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">并推动安全认证和安全检测结果互认</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">避免重复认证</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">检测</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第二十四条 </span></b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"> 网络运营者为用户办理网络接入</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">域名注册服务</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">办理固定电话</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">移动电话等入网手续</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">或者为用户提供信息发布</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">即时通讯等服务</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">在与用户签订协议或者确认提供服务时</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">应当要求用户提供真实身份信息</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">用户不提供真实身份信息的</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">网络运营者不得为其提供相关服务</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.5pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">国家实施网络可信身份战略</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">支持研究开发安全</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">方便的电子身份认证技术</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">推动不同电子身份认证之间的互认</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第二十五条 </span></b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"> 网络运营者应当制定网络安全事件应急预案</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">及时处置系统漏洞</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">计算机病毒</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">网络攻击</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">网络侵入等安全风险</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">；</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">在发生危害网络安全的事件时</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">立即启动应急预案</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">采取相应的补救措施</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">并按照规定向有关主管部门报告</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第二十六条</span></b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">  开展网络安全认证</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">检测</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">风险评估等活动</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">向社会发布系统漏洞</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">计算机病毒</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">网络攻击</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">网络侵入等网络安全信息</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">应当遵守国家有关规定</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第二十七条</span></b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">  任何个人和组织不得从事非法侵入他人网络</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">干扰他人网络正常功能</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">窃取网络数据等危害网络安全的活动</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">；</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">不得提供专门用于从事侵入网络</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">干扰网络正常功能及防护措施</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">窃取网络数据等危害网络安全活动的程序</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">工具</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">；</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">明知他人从事危害网络安全的活动的</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体;
