FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">不得为其提供技术支持</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">广告推广</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">支付结算等帮助</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第二十八条</span></b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">  网络运营者应当为公安机关</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">国家安全机关依法维护国家安全和侦查犯罪的活动提供技术支持和协助</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第二十九条</span></b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">  国家支持网络运营者之间在网络安全信息收集</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">分析</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">通报和应急处置等方面进行合作</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">提高网络运营者的安全保障能力</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.5pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">有关行业组织建立健全本行业的网络安全保护规范和协作机制</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">加强对网络安全风险的分析评估</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">定期向会员进行风险警示</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">支持</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">协助会员应对网络安全风险</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第三十条</span></b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">  网信部门和有关部门在履行网络安全保护职责中获取的信息</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">只能用于维护网络安全的需要</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">不得用于其他用途</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: center; mso-layout-grid-align: none" class="MsoNormal" align="center"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 华文楷体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZKTK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"><font face="楷体_GB2312">第二节 关键信息基础设施的运行安全<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></font></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第三十一条</span></b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">  国家对公共通信和信息服务</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">能源</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">交通</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">水利</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">金融</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">公共服务</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">电子政务等重要行业和领域</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">以及其他一旦遭到破坏</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">丧失功能或者数据泄露</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">可能严重危害国家安全</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">国计民生</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">公共利益的关键信息基础设施</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">在网络安全等级保护制度的基础上</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">实行重点保护</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">关键信息基础设施的具体范围和安全保护办法由国务院制定</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.5pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">国家鼓励关键信息基础设施以外的网络运营者自愿参与关键信息基础设施保护体系</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第三十二条 </span></b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"> 按照国务院规定的职责分工</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">负责关键信息基础设施安全保护工作的部门分别编制并组织实施本行业</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">本领域的关键信息基础设施安全规划</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">指导和监督关键信息基础设施运行安全保护工作</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第三十三条</span></b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">  建设关键信息基础设施应当确保其具有支持业务稳定</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">持续运行的性能</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">并保证安全技术措施同步规划</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">同步建设</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">同步使用</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第三十四条</span></b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">  除本法第二十一条的规定外</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">关键信息基础设施的运营者还应当履行下列安全保护义务</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">：<span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">（</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">一</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">）</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">设置专门安全管理机构和安全管理负责人</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">并对该负</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">责人和关键岗位的人员进行安全背景审查</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">；<span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">（</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">二</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">）</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">定期对从业人员进行网络安全教育</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">技术培训和技能</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">考核</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">；<span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">（</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">三</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">）</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">对重要系统和数据库进行容灾备份</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">；<span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">（</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">四</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">）</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">制定网络安全事件应急预案</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">并定期进行演练</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">；<span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">（</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">五</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">）</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">法律</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">行政法规规定的其他义务</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 24.1pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第三十五条 </span></b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"> 关键信息基础设施的运营者采购网络产品和服务</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">可能影响国家安全的</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">应当通过国家网信部门会同国务院有关部门组织的国家安全审查</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第三十六条</span></b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">  关键信息基础设施的运营者采购网络产品和服务</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">应当按照规定与提供者签订安全保密协议</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">明确安全和保密义务与责任</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第三十七条 </span></b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"> 关键信息基础设施的运营者在中华人民共和国境内运营中收集和产生的个人信息和重要数据应当在境内存储</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">因业务需要</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">确需向境外提供的</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">应当按照国家网信部门会同国务院有关部门制定的办法进行安全评估</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">；</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">法律</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">行政法规另有规定的</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">依照其规定</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第三十八条</span></b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">  关键信息基础设施的运营者应当自行或者委托网络安全服务机构对其网络的安全性和可能存在的风险每年至少进行一次检测评估</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">并将检测评估情况和改进措施报送相关负责关键信息基础设施安全保护工作的部门</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第三十九条</span></b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">  国家网信部门应当统筹协调有关部门对关键信息基础设施的安全保护采取下列措施</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">：<span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">（</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">一</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">）</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">对关键信息基础设施的安全风险进行抽查检测</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">提出改进措施</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">必要时可以委托网络安全服务机构对网络存在的安全风险进行检测评估</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">；<span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">（</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">二</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">）</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">定期组织关键信息基础设施的运营者进行网络安全应急演练</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">提高应对网络安全事件的水平和协同配合能力</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">；<span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">（</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">三</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">）</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">促进有关部门</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">关键信息基础设施的运营者以及有关研究机构</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">网络安全服务机构等之间的网络安全信息共享</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">；<span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">（</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">四</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">）</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">对网络安全事件的应急处置与网络功能的恢复等</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">提供技术支持和协助</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: center; mso-layout-grid-align: none" class="MsoNormal" align="center"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第四章  网络信息安全<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></b></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第四十条 </span></b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"> 网络运营者应当对其收集的用户信息严格保密</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">并建立健全用户信息保护制度</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第四十一条 </span></b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"> 网络运营者收集</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">使用个人信息</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">应当遵循合法</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">正当</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">必要的原则</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">公开收集</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">使用规则</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">明示收集</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">使用信息的目的</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">方式和范围</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">并经被收集者同意</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.5pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">网络运营者不得收集与其提供的服务无关的个人信息</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">不得违反法律</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">行政法规的规定和双方的约定收集</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">使用个人信息</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">并应当依照法律</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">行政法规的规定和与用户的约定</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">处理其保存的个人信息</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第四十二条</span></b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">  网络运营者不得泄露</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">篡改</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">毁损其收集的个人信息</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">；</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">未经被收集者同意</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">不得向他人提供个人信息</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">但是</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">经过处理无法识别特定个人且不能复原的除外</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.5pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">网络运营者应当采取技术措施和其他必要措施</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">确保其收集的个人信息安全</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">防止信息泄露</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">毁损</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">丢失</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">在发生或者可能发生个人信息泄露</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">毁损</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">丢失的情况时</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">应当立即采取补救措施</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">按照规定及时告知用户并向有关主管部门报告</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第四十三条</span></b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">  个人发现网络运营者违反法律</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">行政法规的规定或者双方的约定收集</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">使用其个人信息的</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">有权要求网络运营者删除其个人信息</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">；</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">发现网络运营者收集</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">存储的其个人信息有错误的</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">有权要求网络运营者予以更正</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">网络运营者应当采取措施予以删除或者更正</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第四十四条</span></b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">  任何个人和组织不得窃取或者以其他非法方式获取个人信息</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">不得非法出售或者非法向他人提供个人信息</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第四十五条</span></b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">  依法负有网络安全监督管理职责的部门及其工作人员</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">必须对在履行职责中知悉的个人信息</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">隐私和商业秘密严格保密</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">不得泄露</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">出售或者非法向他人提供</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第四十六条</span></b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">  任何个人和组织应当对其使用网络的行为负责</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">不得设立用于实施诈骗</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">传授犯罪方法</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">制作或者销售违禁物品</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">管制物品等违法犯罪活动的网站</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">通讯群组</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">不得利用网络发布涉及实施诈骗</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">制作或者销售违禁物品</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">管制物品以及其他违法犯罪活动的信息</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第四十七条</span></b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">  网络运营者应当加强对其用户发布的信息的管理</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">发现法律</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">行政法规禁止发布或者传输的信息的</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">应当立即停止传输该信息</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">采取消除等处置措施</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">防止信息扩散</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">保存有关记录</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">并向有关主管部门报告</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第四十八条 </span></b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"> 任何个人和组织发送的电子信息</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">提供的应用软件</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">不得设置恶意程序</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">不得含有法律</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">行政法规禁止发布或者传输的信息</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.5pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">电子信息发送服务提供者和应用软件下载服务提供者</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">应当履行安全管理义务</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">知道其用户有前款规定行为的</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">应当停止提供服务</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">采取消除等处置措施</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">保存有关记录</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">并向有关主管部门报告</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第四十九条 </span></b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"> 网络运营者应当建立网络信息安全投诉</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">举报制度</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">公布投诉</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">举报方式等信息</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">及时受理并处理有关网络信息安全的投诉和举报</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.5pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">网络运营者对网信部门和有关部门依法实施的监督检查</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">应当予以配合</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第五十条</span></b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">  国家网信部门和有关部门依法履行网络信息安全监督管理职责</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">发现法律</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">行政法规禁止发布或者传输的信息的</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">应当要求网络运营者停止传输</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">采取消除等处置措施</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">保存有关记录</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">；</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">对来源于中华人民共和国境外的上述信息</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">应当通知有关机构采取技术措施和其他必要措施阻断传播</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: center; mso-layout-grid-align: none" class="MsoNormal" align="center"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第五章  监测预警与应急处置<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></b></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第五十一条</span></b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">  国家建立网络安全监测预警和信息通报制度</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">国家网信部门应当统筹协调有关部门加强网络安全信息收集</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">分析和通报工作</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">按照规定统一发布网络安全监测预警信息</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第五十二条</span></b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">  负责关键信息基础设施安全保护工作的部门</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">应当建立健全本行业</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">本领域的网络安全监测预警和信息通报制度</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">并按照规定报送网络安全监测预警信息</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BX; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第五十三条</span></b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">  国家网信部门协调有关部门建立健全网络安全风险评估和应急工作机制</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">制定网络安全事件应急预案</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">并定期组织演练</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.5pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">负责关键信息基础设施安全保护工作的部门应当制定本行业</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">本领域的网络安全事件应急预案</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">并定期组织演练</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.5pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">网络安全事件应急预案应当按照事件发生后的危害程度</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">影响范围等因素对网络安全事件进行分级</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">并规定相应的应急处置措施</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第五十四条</span></b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">  网络安全事件发生的风险增大时</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">省级以上人民政府有关部门应当按照规定的权限和程序</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">并根据网络安全风险的特点和可能造成的危害</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">采取下列措施</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">：<span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">（</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">一</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">）</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">要求有关部门</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">机构和人员及时收集</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">报告有关信息</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">加强对网络安全风险的监测</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">；<span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">（</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">二</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">）</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">组织有关部门</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">机构和专业人员</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">对网络安全风险信息进行分析评估</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">预测事件发生的可能性</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">影响范围和危害程度</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">；<span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">（</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">三</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">）</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">向社会发布网络安全风险预警</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">发布避免</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">减轻危害的措施</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第五十五条</span></b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">  发生网络安全事件</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">应当立即启动网络安全事件应急预案</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">对网络安全事件进行调查和评估</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">要求网络运营者采取技术措施和其他必要措施</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">消除安全隐患</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">防止危害扩大</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">并及时向社会发布与公众有关的警示信息</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第五十六条 </span></b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"> 省级以上人民政府有关部门在履行网络安全监督管理职责中</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">发现网络存在较大安全风险或者发生安全事件的</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">可以按照规定的权限和程序对该网络的运营者的法定代表人或者主要负责人进行约谈</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">网络运营者应当按照要求采取措施</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">进行整改</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">消除隐患</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第五十七条 </span></b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"> 因网络安全事件</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">发生突发事件或者生产安全事故的</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">应当依照</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">《</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">中华人民共和国突发事件应对法</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">》、《</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">中华人民共和国安全生产法</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">》</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">等有关法律</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">行政法规的规定处置</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第五十八条</span></b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"> 因维护国家安全和社会公共秩序</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">处置重大突发社会安全事件的需要</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">经国务院决定或者批准</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">可以在特定区域对网络通信采取限制等临时措施</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: center; mso-layout-grid-align: none" class="MsoNormal" align="center"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体">第六章  法律责任<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第五十九条</span></b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">  网络运营者不履行本法第二十一条</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第二十五条规定的网络安全保护义务的</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">由有关主管部门责令改正</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">给予警告</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">；</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">拒不改正或者导致危害网络安全等后果的</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">处一万元以上十万元以下罚款</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">对直接负责的主管人员处五千元以上五万元以下罚款</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.5pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">关键信息基础设施的运营者不履行本法第三十三条</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体;
