FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第三十四条</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第三十六条</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第三十八条规定的网络安全保护义务的</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">由有关主管部门责令改正</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">给予警告</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">；</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">拒不改正或者导致危害网络安全等后果的</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">处十万元以上一百万元以下罚款</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">对直接负责的主管人员处一万元以上十万元以下罚款</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第六十条</span></b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">  违反本法第二十二条第一款</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第二款和第四十八条第一款规定</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">有下列行为之一的</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">由有关主管部门责令改正</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">给予警告</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">；</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">拒不改正或者导致危害网络安全等后果的</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">处五万元以上五十万元以下罚款</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">对直接负责的主管人员处一万元以上十万元以下罚款</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">：<span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">（</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">一</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">）</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">设置恶意程序的</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">；<span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">（</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">二</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">）</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">对其产品</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">服务存在的安全缺陷</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">漏洞等风险未立即采取补救措施</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">或者未按照规定及时告知用户并向有关主管部门报告的</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">；<span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">（</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">三</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">）</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">擅自终止为其产品</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">服务提供安全维护的</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第六十一条</span></b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">  网络运营者违反本法第二十四条第一款规定</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">未要求用户提供真实身份信息</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">或者对不提供真实身份信息的用户提供相关服务的</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">由有关主管部门责令改正</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">；</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">拒不改正或者情节严重的</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">处五万元以上五十万元以下罚款</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">并可以由有关主管部门责令暂停相关业务</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">停业整顿</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">关闭网站</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">吊销相关业务许可证或者吊销营业执照</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">对直接负责的主管人员和其他直接责任人员处一万元以上十万元以下罚款</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第六十二条 </span></b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"> 违反本法第二十六条规定</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">开展网络安全认证</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">检测</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">风险评估等活动</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">或者向社会发布系统漏洞</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">计算机病毒</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">网络攻击</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">网络侵入等网络安全信息的</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">由有关主管部门责令改正</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">给予警告</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">；</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">拒不改正或者情节严重的</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">处一万元以上十万元以下罚款</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">并可以由有关主管部门责令暂停相关业务</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">停业整顿</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">关闭网站</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">吊销相关业务许可证或者吊销营业执照</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">对直接负责的主管人员和其他直接责任人员处五千元以上五万元以下罚款</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第六十三条</span></b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">  违反本法第二十七条规定</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">从事危害网络安全的活动</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">或者提供专门用于从事危害网络安全活动的程序</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">工具</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">或者为他人从事危害网络安全的活动提供技术支持</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">广告推广</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">支付结算等帮助</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">尚不构成犯罪的</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">由公安机关没收违法所得</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">处五日以下拘留</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">可以并处五万元以上五十万元以下罚款</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">；</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">情节较重的</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">处五日以上十五日以下拘留</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">可以并处十万元以上一百万元以下罚款</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.5pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">单位有前款行为的</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">由公安机关没收违法所得</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">处十万元以上一百万元以下罚款</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">并对直接负责的主管人员和其他直接责任人员依照前款规定处罚</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.5pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">违反本法第二十七条规定</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">受到治安管理处罚的人员</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">五年内不得从事网络安全管理和网络运营关键岗位的工作</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">；</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">受到刑事处罚的人员</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">终身不得从事网络安全管理和网络运营关键岗位的工作</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第六十四条 </span></b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"> 网络运营者</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">网络产品或者服务的提供者违反本法第二十二条第三款</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第四十一条至第四十三条规定</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">侵害个人信息依法得到保护的权利的</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">由有关主管部门责令改正</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">可以根据情节单处或者并处警告</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">没收违法所得</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">处违法所得一倍以上十倍以下罚款</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">没有违法所得的</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">处一百万元以下罚款</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">对直接负责的主管人员和其他直接责任人员处一万元以上十万元以下罚款</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">；</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">情节严重的</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">并可以责令暂停相关业务</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">停业整顿</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">关闭网站</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">吊销相关业务许可证或者吊销营业执照</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.5pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">违反本法第四十四条规定</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">窃取或者以其他非法方式获取</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">非法出售或者非法向他人提供个人信息</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">尚不构成犯罪的</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">由公安机关没收违法所得</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">并处违法所得一倍以上十倍以下罚款</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">没有违法所得的</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">处一百万元以下罚款</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第六十五条</span></b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">  关键信息基础设施的运营者违反本法第三十五条规定</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">使用未经安全审查或者安全审查未通过的网络产品或者服务的</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">由有关主管部门责令停止使用</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">处采购金额一倍以上十倍以下罚款</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">；</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">对直接负责的主管人员和其他直接责任人员处一万元以上十万元以下罚款</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第六十六条</span></b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">  关键信息基础设施的运营者违反本法第三十七条规定</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">在境外存储网络数据</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">或者向境外提供网络数据的</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">由有关主管部门责令改正</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">给予警告</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">没收违法所得</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">处五万元以上五十万元以下罚款</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">并可以责令暂停相关业务</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">停业整顿</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">关闭网站</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">吊销相关业务许可证或者吊销营业执照</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">；</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">对直接负责的主管人员和其他直接责任人员处一万元以上十万元以下罚款</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第六十七条</span></b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">  违反本法第四十六条规定</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">设立用于实施违法犯罪活动的网站</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">通讯群组</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">或者利用网络发布涉及实施违法犯罪活动的信息</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">尚不构成犯罪的</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">由公安机关处五日以下拘留</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">可以并处一万元以上十万元以下罚款</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">；</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">情节较重的</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">处五日以上十五日以下拘留</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">可以并处五万元以上五十万元以下罚款</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">关闭用于实施违法犯罪活动的网站</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">通讯群组</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.5pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">单位有前款行为的</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">由公安机关处十万元以上五十万元以下罚款</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">并对直接负责的主管人员和其他直接责任人员依照前款规定处罚</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第六十八条 </span></b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"> 网络运营者违反本法第四十七条规定</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">对法律</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">行政法规禁止发布或者传输的信息未停止传输</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">采取消除等处置措施</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">保存有关记录的</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">由有关主管部门责令改正</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">给予警告</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">没收违法所得</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">；</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">拒不改正或者情节严重的</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">处十万元以上五十万元以下罚款</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">并可以责令暂停相关业务</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">停业整顿</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">关闭网站</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">吊销相关业务许可证或者吊销营业执照</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">对直接负责的主管人员和其他直接责任人员处一万元以上十万元以下罚款</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.5pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">电子信息发送服务提供者</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">应用软件下载服务提供者</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">不履行本法第四十八条第二款规定的安全管理义务的</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">依照前款规定处罚</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第六十九条</span></b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">  网络运营者违反本法规定</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">有下列行为之一的</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">由有关主管部门责令改正</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">；</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">拒不改正或者情节严重的</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">处五万元以上五十万元以下罚款</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">对直接负责的主管人员和其他直接责任人员</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">处一万元以上十万元以下罚款</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">：<span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">（</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">一</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">）</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">不按照有关部门的要求对法律</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">行政法规禁止发布或</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">者传输的信息</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">采取停止传输</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">消除等处置措施的</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">；</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BX; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US"> <span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">（</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">二</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">）</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">拒绝</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">阻碍有关部门依法实施的监督检查的</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">；<span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">（</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">三</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">）</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">拒不向公安机关</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">国家安全机关提供技术支持和协助的</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第七十条 </span></b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"> 发布或者传输本法第十二条第二款和其他法律</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">行政法规禁止发布或者传输的信息的</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">依照有关法律</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">行政法规的规定处罚</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第七十一条</span></b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">  有本法规定的违法行为的</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">依照有关法律</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">行政法规的规定记入信用档案</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">并予以公示</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第七十二条 </span></b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"> 国家机关政务网络的运营者不履行本法规定的网络安全保护义务的</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">由其上级机关或者有关机关责令改正</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">；</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">对直接负责的主管人员和其他直接责任人员依法给予处分</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第七十三条 </span></b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt"> 网信部门和有关部门违反本法第三十条规定</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">将在履行网络安全保护职责中获取的信息用于其他用途的</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">对直接负责的主管人员和其他直接责任人员依法给予处分</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.5pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">网信部门和有关部门的工作人员玩忽职守</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">滥用职权</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">徇私舞弊</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">尚不构成犯罪的</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">依法给予处分</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第七十四条</span></b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">  违反本法规定</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">给他人造成损害的</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">依法承担民事责任</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.5pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">违反本法规定</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">构成违反治安管理行为的</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">依法给予治安管理处罚</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">；</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">构成犯罪的</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">依法追究刑事责任</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第七十五条</span></b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">  境外的机构</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">组织</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">个人从事攻击</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">侵入</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">干扰</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">破坏等危害中华人民共和国的关键信息基础设施的活动</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">造成严重后果的</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">依法追究法律责任</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">；</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">国务院公安部门和有关部门并可以决定对该机构</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">组织</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">个人采取冻结财产或者其他必要的制裁措施</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: center; mso-layout-grid-align: none" class="MsoNormal" align="center"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体">第七章  附    则<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第七十六条</span></b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">  本法下列用语的含义</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">：<span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">（</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">一</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">）</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">网络</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">是指由计算机或者其他信息终端及相关设备组成的按照一定的规则和程序对信息进行收集</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">存储</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">传输</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">交换</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">处理的系统</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">（</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">二</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">）</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">网络安全</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">是指通过采取必要措施</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">防范对网络的攻击</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">侵入</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">干扰</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">破坏和非法使用以及意外事故</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">使网络处于稳定可靠运行的状态</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">以及保障网络数据的完整性</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">保密性</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">可用性的能力</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">（</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">三</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">）</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">网络运营者</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">是指网络的所有者</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">管理者和网络服务提供者</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">（</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">四</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">）</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">网络数据</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">是指通过网络收集</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">存储</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">传输</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">处理和产生的各种电子数据</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">（</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">五</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">）</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">个人信息</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">是指以电子或者其他方式记录的能够单独或者与其他信息结合识别自然人个人身份的各种信息</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">包括但不限于自然人的姓名</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">出生日期</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">身份证件号码</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">个人生物识别信息</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">住址</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">电话号码等</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第七十七条</span></b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">  存储</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">处理涉及国家秘密信息的网络的运行安全保护</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">除应当遵守本法外</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">还应当遵守保密法律</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">、</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">行政法规的规定</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第七十八条</span></b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">  军事网络的安全保护</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">，</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">由中央军事委员会另行规定</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。<span lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: distribute; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt; mso-char-indent-count: 1.96" class="MsoNormal" align="justify"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">第七十九条</span></b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">  本法自</span><span st="on" year="2017" month="6" day="1" islunardate="False" isrocdate="False"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">2017</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">年</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">6</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">月</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt" lang="EN-US">1</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">日起</span></span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: FZFSK--GBK1-0; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">施行</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: E-BZ; mso-font-kerning: 0pt">。</span><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-SIZE: 12pt" lang="EN-US"><span></span></span></p><!--/enpcontent--></div>
